< Review>
First time going to Stumptown and to be honest I was a little disappointed. If you are looking for a fun little spot to grab a beer with a buddy this is the place for you. The patio area was really nice over looking the river. Due to COVID we had to order our food at the door (the food was way too pricey for what you got) and then pick it up at a different window. We also had to clean out dishes and table before we left. My husband and I got the pulled pork sandwich and the polish dog to share together and both were not good at all. On the menu it said that pork was smoked for 12 hours, I don't know what happened in those 12 hours but it had no flavor and was dry (even with coleslaw on it). Thank God the beer was good and the staff was friendly.</Review>

Funky Russian River brewery/bar.  The inside is dark and reminds me of an English pub, but the outside has a great covered eating/drinking area with air hocky tables.  There is a fabulous patio with views of the Russian River.  On Monday nights a special caterer comes in and provides a wonderful barbeque, and soul food dinner.  Ribs, collar greens, mac n cheese, sausage.  Delicious!  On other nights Wood fired pizza is available.  Really good micro brews.  if you are into paddle sports. you can paddle down the RR and stop beach your craft on the brewery's shore and come in for a drink or food.< /text>

<text>Absolutely stunning setting. This had the potential to be a great experience but it was spoiled by the insolent Australian member of staff.

On arrival, we walked through the pub to reach the beer garden, with our dog (a service animal). With no greeting or any respect he marched up and shouted at us for bringing an animal into a bar and told us we should've gone through the side entrance. We stopped in our tracks, speechless. He then ordered us to continue through because we've already come this far.

The beer garden has such a stunning view over the river that we decided to ignore this man. My wife joined the queue for the bar where there's a sign up that says couples have to use the stools and not take up space at the tables, so I chose a pair of stools overlooking the river.

When my wife came back with the drinks she said she'd rather sit in the shade, if possible. Despite there being plenty of shaded seating around the large (mostly empty) tables, I didn't want to get shouted at again so decided to shift the pair of stools a few feet to the right, so they're in the shade. The Ozzy t**t must've been watching our every move because before I even lifted the first stool he aggressively shouted, "DON'T MOVE THE FURNITURE!". Seriously?

I calmly approached him and asked what the solution should be, since we want to sit in the shade but the sign says we have to sit on stools. He unapologetically directed us to sit at the tables and ignore the sign. Wait, so now it's ok to ignore signs?

By this point we just wanted to drink our drinks and get the hell out of there before I lost my temper with this a-hole. Having read some of the other one-star reviews I can see that other people had a similar experience with him.

We would definitely go back, if he wasn't working there.<//text></record></dataset><record>

<text>Stumptown Brewery is as local as it gets for local beer. And not many breweries have a separate yard where your dog can hangout while you have a beverage... Or a place to pull up from the river and eat lunch and keep paddling - or dinner when you're done for the day - a cold beer is awfully good sounding when you are headed down the river. Stumptown has all of the above.

The food is bar food and cash only. Burgers, fries, onion rings, and such.

The back deck is extensive and awesome for hanging out and looking at the river... And the lower lawn is home to the annual Beer Revival and BBQ cook off.</text><user>114596361411457591114< /user>< Response>

To our surprise they fit us in without a reservation but said nothing was available on the patio. Once seated in the bustling dining room we were told a patio table had become available so we moved. <rate>1</rate>< Text>
Myself and a friend went to dinner here last week. I asked our server if they had anything that accommodates a vegan diet, and he literally told me if I wanted to eat something vegan I could go elsewhere. Even typing that sounds so extreme it sounds like it's made up.

When I pressed more, he said something on the menu was gluten free if that helped. So clearly he doesn't understand what vegan is. I asked to talk to someone else just because it didn't seem like he was understanding what I was asking. He said no one else at the restaurant could help me. I should have just left right then but it was getting late and things tend to close early around there and my friend had already ordered.

So I got what was described on the menu as just pasta and tomato sauce. When it was served to me, it had a lot of cheese on top, so I couldn't eat it.

Trying to reason with our server was definitely not going to happen based on the long conversation we had with him resisting any attempt to try to help me find something to eat in the restaurant. So I paid the ***$28*** for some pasta I couldn't even eat.

So rather than posting a passive aggressive yelp review, I called the restaurant the next day and asked to speak to a manager. I told him the story, he seemed surprised by the servers actions which was reassuring. He offered to give me a free meal next time and said they offer prepared vegetables for vegans (something our server didn't offer) and I could come back whenever. But I don't live near there so I wouldn't have been coming back any time soon. I asked if he could just refund me for the meal. He took my number and said he wasn't sure that he could but if he could refund me the meal he would. (How would it not be possible to issue a refund?)

He never called me back. So I've disputed the charge on my credit card. I really dread the idea of having to pay $28 to be mocked by a server and then left hungry the rest of the night.

I've been vegan for a long time and I've never had a restaurant not be able to serve me, especially one that has the perception of being upscale. Big bummer. Hopefully the manager is reading this and can finally give me my refund. Sorry to write the bad review but it seems to be the only way to possibly get someone's attention.</Text>

<UserId.>115442520938810454944< /UserId.><name>Lisa<//name><time>1466711745257<//time>< Rate>

< text>
Hands down best meal.  This is a fairly new restaurant for Ojai, situated within an adorable house.  The outside porch is definitely the seat you want to try and grab, as the views of the mountains are beautiful while eating.  The food is exquisite - nothing like it around.  Very high end, authentic, Italian food with an unbelievable creative twist in sauces and fillings.  All of the pastas are home made.  Not your run of the mill Italian menu, so if you are looking for "spaghetti and meatballs" this is not for you.

The Owner/Chef, Pietro, takes a hands on approach to the restaurant.  You'll see him touring the tables and chatting with each guest.  It really makes for a delightful, special dinner experience.

The wait staff is extremely attentive, even during busy nights.

The word is getting out because each time we go it is more crowded!<//text>

Had high hopes for this place. I believe this is the Big Fish in the Small Pond that is Ojai -- would not last a year in a more competitive food market. Had an appetizer, two pasta dishes, a couple of glasses of wine and a kid-sized pasta along with a dessert. Both pasta dishes were under-seasoned, with one being good and the other being just bland -- no kidding, it was flavorless. As someone else described earlier, the featured ingredients of the dish were miniscule. Perhaps 10 tiny cubes of squash and a sprinkling of mushrooms incorporated into the dish. The plating is straight out of the 90s with criss-crossed reductions and sauces on every plate that could accommodate it. The dessert took 30 minutes to reach our table, by which time we had already finished our coffee. I will say our servers were friendly, but maybe tuned-out. If you're looking for a cool space under the guise of fine dining with some friends, by all means check the place out. But bring your patience and some salt.<//Text>

Siciliana Pizza...

I have been a frequent customer at this lakefront location and restaurant in the city of Mission Viejo. Every time I have tasted the Sicilian pizza they make there, which is characterized by a high dough of about 2 inches and sometimes even taller. Unfortunately, for some time now, the quality of the dough has gone down a lot and its height does not exceed an inch or something. The last time I ordered it, I was very disappointed. I think they do it to reduce costs, but I prefer to pay about 5 dollars more but take the usual quality. I won't order it anymore because I don't think I'll come back there. Perhaps in another location they maintain the same quality of pizza, but in front of the Lake of Mission Viejo, no longer. Regards!  (The service is still very good as always)...< /Text>

We ordered a few things to sample, ravioli with lobster, cioppino, caprese, and a pizza. <Review>I've been on a search for the past 7 years, to find a quality barber, barber shop, and business that I wanted to return to every 2 weeks to get a hair cut.

I've been downtown, at the north end of town,, at the south end of town, all near campus, everywhere..... searching.  I've found my home. The last barbershop I went to downtown left my pocketbook hurting, and feeling as if I wasn't welcome.

The wife told me about a patron who frequents where she works was opening a shop and that I should go check it out.  I called this morning and was told they close at 5... I get off at 5.  Miguel told me to come straight over after work and he'd get me taken care of.

Edwin was my barber and this young man gives me hope for the future of barbers and the future of how pride shows in their craft.  Miguel has obviously done his due diligence in bringing on the best talent paired with the best customer service.  I may be 39, but I walked out feeling like a 21 year old ready to tear up the town.

I told Edwin the look I was going for, then he showed me a picture of a haircut he had done and I was like "YES!!!! THATS IT!"

Honestly as long as I live in chico, this is the one and only barbershop I will be a patron of.  I would STRONGLY suggest that all the others emulate Miguel and his business as the perfect way to run a barbershop in chico.< /Review><pics>None< /pics><resp>None<//resp><gmapID>0x8082d8e8700d7197:0x8289cde69284de06</gmapID></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
Gorgeous Nature atmosphere. Surrounded by houses so its a great place to have fun with the family. Childrens play area, park benches, basketball, tennis courts, and small walking trails for seniors.Limeted bbq areas. Lots of grassy areas. Clean park. Make sure your car is registered and drive a safe speed. The sheriff and local police patrol and frequent the park regularly for safety. They will cite you so follow all the rules!! Residents have a neighborhood park watch and have no problems calling the police for disturbances, excessive alcohol or marijuana smoking. This is park for family, children, and senior events.<//Review>

< review>
This was my first and only time trying Church's Chicken. My time living in California was limited. We decided to try the Smokehouse Chicken because it was on special and being promoted, at the time. It was so so delicious. A little overcooked, but the flavor made up for in. I'm also not a real biscuit fan, but their biscuits... are so 'Oh My God' mouthwatering! We tried to get more Smokehouse chicken a few days later, but they ran out. The service at the drive-thru was really great. The lady was really patient with us first-timers and she even made us laugh. I'd definitely frequent Church's Chicken when I return to California.</review>
